       <article class="post-2720 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-entree category-healthy category-new-year category-soup category-vegetarian tag-avocado tag-corn tag-quinoa tag-tomato wpautop entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
          Quinoa Chili
         </h1>
         <p class="entry-meta">
          <time class="entry-time" datetime="2013-10-16T21:34:18+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
           October 16, 2013
          </time>
          by
          <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
           <a class="entry-author-link" href="/author/damndeliciousbloggmail-com/" itemprop="url" rel="author">
            <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
             Chungah
            </span>
           </a>
          </span>
          <span class="entry-comments-link">
           <a href="#comments">
            154 Comments
           </a>
          </span>
         </p>
        </header>
        <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
         <div class="pin-it-btn-wrapper">
          <a data-pin-color="gray" data-pin-config="beside" data-pin-do="buttonBookmark" href="//www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdamndelicious.net%2F2013%2F10%2F16%2Fquinoa-chili%2F&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2Fdamndelicious.net%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F10%2FQuinoa-Chili.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa%20Chili%20-%20This%20vegetarian%2C%20protein-packed%20chili%20is%20the%20perfect%20bowl%20of%20comfort%20food%20that%20you%20can%20eat%20guilt-free%21" rel="nobox">
           <img data-pib-button="true" src="//assets.pinterest.com/images/pidgets/pin_it_button.png" title="Pin It"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <p style="text-align: center;">
          <em>
           This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6376 aligncenter" height="975" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/Quinoa-Chili.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/Quinoa-Chili.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          Its been a bit warm here in San Francisco but Ive been wanting to make chili for weeks now. Chili gives me the perfect excuse to have oh-so-crumbly cornbread on the side, except I overdo it and make it a main course. Either way, I still wanted a piping hot bowl of chili. Desperately. But this time, I tried something very different with my batch of chili  I added
          <strong>
           quinoa
          </strong>
          , and lots of it!
         </p>
         <p>
          <span id="more-2720">
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6371 aligncenter" height="433" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3904edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3904edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6367 aligncenter" height="431" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3905edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3905edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6372 aligncenter" height="426" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3908edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3908edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6368 aligncenter" height="420" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3911edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3911edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6369 aligncenter" height="426" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3914edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3914edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6370 aligncenter" height="432" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3916edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3916edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6366 aligncenter" height="429" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3917edit1.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3917edit1.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          The quinoa added such a fun texture, soaking up all the flavors and goodness of this chili. Its also loaded with kidney beans, black beans, tons of veggies and just enough lime juice to give you a subtle kick in the pants. Plus, this batch will make enough to feed an army so itll keep you and your family well fed for days!
         </p>
         <p>
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="Quinoa Chili - This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!" class="size-full wp-image-6378 aligncenter" height="975" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3938edit.jpg" width="650"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://damndelicious.net/2013/10/16/quinoa-chili/&amp;media=http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/IMG_3938edit.jpg&amp;description=Quinoa Chili')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <div class="zlrecipe-container-border" id="zlrecipe-container-123">
          <div class="serif zlrecipe" id="zlrecipe-container" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">
           <div id="zlrecipe-innerdiv">
            <div class="item b-b">
             <div class="zlrecipe-print-link fl-r">
              <a class="print-link" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="zlrPrint('zlrecipe-container-123', 'http://damndelicious.net/wp-content/plugins/ziplist-recipe-plugin/'); return false" title="Print this recipe">
               <img src="/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/print-recipe-all-caps.png"/>
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="zl-recipe-link fl-r zl-rmvd" id="zl-recipe-link-123">
             </div>
             <div class="b-b h-1 strong" id="zlrecipe-title" itemprop="name">
              Quinoa Chili
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="zlmeta zlclear">
             <div class="fl-l width-50">
              <p id="zlrecipe-prep-time">
               Prep Time
               <span content="PT10M" itemprop="prepTime">
                10 minutes
               </span>
              </p>
              <p id="zlrecipe-cook-time">
               Cook Time
               <span content="PT35M" itemprop="cookTime">
                35 minutes
               </span>
              </p>
              <p id="zlrecipe-total-time">
               Total Time
               <span content="PT45M" itemprop="totalTime">
                45 minutes
               </span>
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="fl-l width-50">
              <p id="zlrecipe-yield">
               Yield
               <span itemprop="recipeYield">
                6 servings
               </span>
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="zlclear">
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="img-desc-wrap">
             <p class="t-a-c hide-card">
              <img alt="Quinoa Chili" class="photo" itemprop="image" src="/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/Quinoa-Chili.jpg" style="width: 180px;" title="Quinoa Chili"/>
             </p>
             <div id="zlrecipe-summary" itemprop="description">
              <p class="summary italic">
               This vegetarian, protein-packed chili is the perfect bowl of comfort food that you can eat guilt-free!
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-ingredients">
             Ingredients
            </p>
            <ul id="zlrecipe-ingredients-list">
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-0" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 cup quinoa
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-1" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 tablespoon olive oil
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-2" itemprop="ingredients">
              3 cloves garlic, minced
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-3" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 onion, diced
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-4" itemprop="ingredients">
              2 (14.5-ounce) cans diced tomatoes
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-5" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 (15-ounce) can tomato sauce
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-6" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 (4.5-ounce) can diced green chiles
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-7" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 1/2 tablespoons chili powder, or more, to taste
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-8" itemprop="ingredients">
              2 teaspoons ground cumin
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-9" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 1/2 teaspoons paprika
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-10" itemprop="ingredients">
              1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-11" itemprop="ingredients">
              Kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper, to taste
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-12" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 (15-ounce) can kidney beans, drained and rinsed
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-13" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 (15-ounce) can black beans, drained and rinsed
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-14" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 1/2 cups corn kernels, frozen, canned or roasted
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-15" itemprop="ingredients">
              3 tablespoons chopped fresh cilantro leaves
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-16" itemprop="ingredients">
              Juice of 1 lime, optional
             </li>
             <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-17" itemprop="ingredients">
              1 avocado, halved, seeded, peeled and diced
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-instructions">
             Instructions
            </p>
            <ul class="instructions" id="zlrecipe-instructions-list">
             <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-0" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
              In a large saucepan of 2 cups water, cook quinoa according to package instructions; set aside.
             </li>
             <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-1" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
              Heat olive oil in a Dutch oven or large pot over medium high heat. Add garlic and onion, and cook, stirring frequently, until onions have become translucent, about 2-3 minutes.
             </li>
             <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-2" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
              Stir in quinoa, diced tomatoes, tomato sauce, green chiles, chili powder, cumin, paprika, cayenne pepper and 1-2 cups water, making sure to cover most of the ingredients; season with salt and pepper, to taste.
             </li>
             <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-3" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
              Reduce heat to low; simmer, covered, until thickened, about 30 minutes. Stir in beans, corn, cilantro and lime juice, if using, until heated through, about 2 minutes.
             </li>
             <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-4" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
              Serve immediately with avocado, if desired.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-notes">
             Notes
            </p>
            <div id="zlrecipe-notes-list">
             <p class="notes">
              Adapted from
              <a href="//www.cookingclassy.com/2013/07/quinoa-chili/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.cookingclassy.com/2013/07/quinoa-chili/', 'Cooking Classy']);">
               Cooking Classy
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="ziplist-recipe-plugin" style="display: none;">
             3.1
            </div>

            </a>

A few people asked about making this in the slow cooker. I make a quinoa chili recipe similar to this one in the slow cooker and it works very well. All the ingredients are put into the slow cooker including uncooked quinoa and I cook on low for 5 &#8211; 7 hours. The quinoa doesn&#8217;t become soggy at all and comes out perfect everytime. I did make a few changes because I needed to put it in the CROCK-POT. So instead of putting in canned beans, I put in dried, unsoaked beans, 1/2 cup kidney and 1/2 cup black beans. Instead of putting in the cooked quinoa, I put in 1/2 cup uncooked quinoa, and I didn&#8217;t have fresh cilantro so I put in 1 tsp. dried cilantro. It takes 5 hours on high and approximately 8 hours on low. Definitely do the avocado and cheese on top.          </header>
         <div class="comment-content" itemprop="commentText">
          <p>
           Made this tonight and it was delicious! Great flavor and consistency, with lots of leftovers.
           <br/>
           Next time may add a little more spice, but loved the lime!
          </p>
         </div>

         <div class="comment-content" itemprop="commentText">

           This is a terrific recipe. I normally make chili with ground turkey, but I honestly dont even miss it now that I have this recipe. Ive made it twice now and I am sure I will make it many more. With my last batch, I forgot to pick up lime juice and green chiles, but it turned out great anyway. If youre even a little in doubt about this recipe, try it anyway! You likely wont regret it. Oh, and it really does make enough to feed an army.
